Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share, effective tax rate, income before income taxes, income tax expense, and net income excluding gains on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the investment gains facilitates an understanding as to the impacts of the investment and the company&#8217;s financial performance.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span><br/></span></div><div --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- Accenture raises all elements of its business outlook for fiscal 2021&#59; now expects full-year revenue growth of 6.5% to 8.5% in local currency&#59; operating margin of 15.0% to 15.1%&#59; GAAP EPS of $8.67 to $8.85&#59; adjusted EPS of $8.32 to $8.50&#59; free cash flow of $7.0 billion to $7.5&#160;billion&#59; and cash returned to shareholders of at least $5.8 billion -- </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; Mar. 18, 2021 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the second quarter of fiscal 2021, ended Feb. 28, 2021, with revenues of $12.1&#160;billion, an increase of 8% in U.S. dollars and 5% in local currency over the same period last year. Revenue growth for the quarter was reduced approximately 2 percentage points by a decline in revenues from reimbursable travel costs. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted earnings per share were $2.23, a 17% increase from $1.91 for the second quarter last year, including gains on an investment of $0.21 and $0.07, respectively. On an adjusted basis, EPS of $2.03 increased 10% from $1.84 for the second quarter last year.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating income was $1.65 billion, an 11% increase over the same period last year, and operating margin was 13.7%, an expansion of 30 basis points.    </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the quarter were a record $16.0 billion, with record bookings in both consulting and outsourcing, at $8.0 billion each.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company also announced a one-time bonus, equal to one week of base pay, for its people below managing director.&#160;This bonus recognizes the exceptional contributions and dedication of all Accenture people to its clients during this challenging year.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, Accenture&#8217;s chief executive officer, said, &#8220;With our outstanding second-quarter financial results, we have returned to overall pre-pandemic growth ahead of expectations while continuing to take market share faster than before the pandemic. We have seen another quarter of strong, broad-</font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">based demand for our services across geographic markets and industries, and delivered record new bookings as well as excellent profitability and free cash flow. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;Our performance reflects the power of our laser focus on creating client value and being a trusted partner, incredibly talented people and unwavering commitment to inclusion and diversity, strong ecosystem partnerships, and the substantial investments we have made year in and year out since we set out to be the leader in digital, cloud and security and continuous innovation. We are proud to be helping our clients not only recover and rebuild but also reimagine their futures.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the second quarter of fiscal 2021 were $12.09&#160;billion, compared with $11.14&#160;billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2020, an increase of 8% in U.S. dollars and 5% in local currency, including a reduction of approximately 2 percentage points from a decline in revenues from reimbursable travel costs. Revenues were approximately $140 million above the top end of the company&#8217;s guided range of $11.55 billion to $11.95 billion. The foreign-exchange impact for the quarter was approximately positive 3%, consistent with the assumption provided in the company&#8217;s first-quarter earnings release. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting revenues for the quarter were $6.44 billion, an increase of 4% in U.S. dollars and 1% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020, including a reduction of approximately 3 percentage points from a decline in revenues from reimbursable travel costs.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Outsourcing revenues were $5.65&#160;billion, an increase of 14% in U.S. dollars and 11% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the quarter were $2.23, a 17% increase from $1.91 for the second  quarter last year, including pre-tax gains on an investment of $151 million, or $0.21 per share, and $53&#160;million, or $0.07 per share, respectively. Excluding these gains, adjusted EPS for the second quarter of fiscal 2021 were $2.03, a 10% increase from $1.84 for the second quarter last year. The $0.19 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.21&#160;increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; and </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 increase from a lower share count&#59;   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">partially offset by</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 decrease from a higher effective tax rate&#59;   </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01&#160;decrease from lower non-operating income&#59; and </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.01 decrease from higher income attributable to noncontrolling interests.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 29.7%, compared with 30.2% for the second quarter last year. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the quarter were $1.94&#160;billion, or 16.1% of revenues, compared with $1.87&#160;billion, or 16.8% of revenues, for the second quarter last year. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating income for the quarter increased 11%, to $1.65 billion, or 13.7% of revenues, compared with $1.49 billion, or 13.4% of revenues, for the second quarter of fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the quarter was 17.1%, compared with 17.1% for the second quarter last year. Excluding the investment gains and the related tax expense of $19&#160;million and $9 </font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">million, respectively, the effective tax rate for the second quarter of fiscal 2021 was 17.5%, compared with 17.1% for the second quarter last year. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Net income for the quarter was $1.46 billion, compared with $1.25 billion for the second quarter last year. Excluding after-tax investment gains of $133 million and $44 million, respectively, net income for the second quarter of fiscal 2021 was $1.33 billion, compared with $1.21 billion for the second quarter last year.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $2.53 billion, and property and equipment additions were $93&#160;million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $2.44 billion. For the same period last year, operating cash flow was $1.53&#160;billion&#59; property and equipment additions were $165&#160;million&#59; and free cash flow was $1.37&#160;billion.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 34 days at Feb. 28, 2021, compared with 35 days at Aug. 31, 2020 and 39 days at Feb. 29, 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at Feb. 28, 2021 was $9.2&#160;billion, compared with $8.4&#160;billion at Aug. 31, 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">New Bookings</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the second quarter were a record $16.0&#160;billion, a 13% increase from the second quarter last year.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Revenues by Geographic Market</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues by geographic market were as follows&#58; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font and local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font 6% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font 11% in U.S. dollars and 9% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Financial Services&#58; $2.38&#160;billion, an increase of 14% in U.S. dollars and 10% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Health &#38; Public Service&#58; $2.26 billion, an increase of 16% in U.S. dollars and 14% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Products&#58; $3.34&#160;billion, an increase of 6% in U.S. dollars and 2% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Returning Cash to Shareholders</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture continues to return cash to shareholders through cash dividends and share repurchases.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Dividend</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On Feb. 12, 2021, a quarterly cash dividend of $0.88 per share was paid to shareholders of record at the close of business on Jan. 14, 2021. These cash dividend payments totaled $561&#160;million, bringing dividend payments for the year to date to $1.12 billion. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture plc has declared another quarterly cash dividend of $0.88 per share for shareholders of record at the close of business on Apr. 15, 2021. This dividend, which is payable on May 14, represents a 10% increase over the quarterly dividend rate of $0.80 per share in fiscal 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Share Repurchase Activity</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">During the second quarter of fiscal 2021, Accenture repurchased or redeemed 4.6&#160;million shares for a total of $1.18 billion, including approximately 2.7 million shares repurchased in the open market. This brings Accenture&#8217;s total share repurchases and redemptions for the first half of fiscal 2021 to 8.0 million shares for a total of $1.95 billion, including approximately 5.5 million shares repurchased in the open market. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s total remaining share repurchase authority at Feb. 28, 2021 was approximately $5.0&#160;billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">At Feb. 28, 2021, Accenture had approximately 636&#160;million total shares outstanding.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Business Outlook</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Third Quarter Fiscal 2021</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture expects revenues for the third quarter of fiscal 2021 to be in the range of $12.55&#160;billion to $12.95&#160;billion, 10% to 13% growth in local currency, reflecting the company&#8217;s assumption of a positive 4.5% foreign-exchange impact compared with the third quarter of fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fiscal Year 2021</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s business outlook for the full 2021 fiscal year continues to assume that the foreign-exchange impact on its results in U.S. dollars will be positive 3% compared with fiscal 2020.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For fiscal 2021, the company now expects revenue growth to be in the range of 6.5% to 8.5% in local currency, compared with 4% to 6% previously, including a reduction of approximately 1&#160;percentage point from a decline in revenues from reimbursable travel costs. </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture now expects operating margin for the full fiscal year to be in the range of 15.0% to 15.1%, compared with 14.8% to 15.0% previously, an expansion of 30 to 40 basis points from fiscal 2020. </font></div><div style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company continues to expect its annual effective tax rate to be in the range of 23.0% to 25.0%.&#160; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company now expects GAAP diluted EPS to be in the range of $8.67 to $8.85, compared with $8.17 to $8.40 previously. Excluding gains on an investment of $0.35 in fiscal 2021 and $0.43 in fiscal 2020, the company expects adjusted fiscal 2021 EPS to be in the range of $8.32 to $8.50, an increase of 12% to 14% over adjusted fiscal 2020 EPS of $7.46. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">For fiscal 2021, the company now expects operating cash flow to be in the range of $7.65 billion to $8.15 billion, compared with $6.65&#160;billion to $7.15&#160;billion previously&#59; continues to expect property and equipment additions to be $650&#160;million&#59; and now expects free cash flow to be in the range of $7.0 billion to $7.5 billion, compared with $6.0 billion to $6.5&#160;billion previously.&#160; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company now expects to return at least $5.8 billion in cash to shareholders through dividends and share repurchases, compared with at least $5.3 billion previously.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Conference Call and Webcast Details</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture will host a conference call at 8&#58;00 a.m. EDT today to discuss its second-quarter financial results.
